2026-05-19T21:37:19.8860650Z [36;1m  echo "$LIPO_OUT" | grep -q "x86_64" || error "Missing x86_64 in $BIN"[0m
2026-05-19T21:37:19.8861200Z [36;1m  echo "$LIPO_OUT" | grep -q "arm64" || error "Missing arm64 in $BIN"[0m
2026-05-19T21:37:19.8861620Z [36;1m[0m
2026-05-19T21:37:19.8861910Z [36;1m  # Binary size check (should be > 1MB for a real plugin)[0m
2026-05-19T21:37:19.8862500Z [36;1m  SIZE=$(stat -f%z "$BIN" 2>/dev/null || stat -c%s "$BIN" 2>/dev/null || echo 0)[0m
2026-05-19T21:37:19.8862970Z [36;1m  if [ "$SIZE" -lt 1048576 ]; then[0m
2026-05-19T21:37:19.8863350Z [36;1m    error "Binary suspiciously small ($SIZE bytes): $BIN"[0m
2026-05-19T21:37:19.8863720Z [36;1m  fi[0m
2026-05-19T21:37:19.8864430Z [36;1m  echo "Binary size: $SIZE bytes"[0m
2026-05-19T21:37:19.8864930Z [36;1mdone[0m
2026-05-19T21:37:19.8865110Z [36;1m[0m
2026-05-19T21:37:19.8865310Z [36;1mecho "Binary architecture: OK"[0m
2026-05-19T21:37:19.8865860Z [36;1m[0m
2026-05-19T21:37:19.8866020Z [36;1m# ============================================================[0m
2026-05-19T21:37:19.8866340Z [36;1m# 4. CODE SIGNATURE INTEGRITY[0m
2026-05-19T21:37:19.8866530Z [36;1m# ============================================================[0m
2026-05-19T21:37:19.8866720Z [36;1mecho ""[0m
2026-05-19T21:37:19.8866840Z [36;1mecho "[4/10] Code Signature Check"[0m
2026-05-19T21:37:19.8867010Z [36;1mecho "----------------------------"[0m
2026-05-19T21:37:19.8867160Z [36;1m[0m
2026-05-19T21:37:19.8867270Z [36;1mfor BUNDLE in "$VST3" "$CLAP"; do[0m
2026-05-19T21:37:19.8867440Z [36;1m  echo "Checking $(basename $BUNDLE)..."[0m
2026-05-19T21:37:19.8867610Z [36;1m[0m
2026-05-19T21:37:19.8867790Z [36;1m  # Strict signature verification (no --deep here, check bundle itself)[0m
2026-05-19T21:37:19.8868130Z [36;1m  codesign -vvv "$BUNDLE" || error "Signature verification failed for $(basename $BUNDLE)"[0m
2026-05-19T21:37:19.8868390Z [36;1m[0m
2026-05-19T21:37:19.8868500Z [36;1m  # Verify signature is ad-hoc[0m
2026-05-19T21:37:19.8868960Z [36;1m  CS_INFO=$(codesign -dvv "$BUNDLE" 2>&1)[0m
2026-05-19T21:37:19.8869160Z [36;1m  echo "$CS_INFO"[0m
2026-05-19T21:37:19.8869410Z [36;1m  echo "$CS_INFO" | grep -q "Signature=adhoc" || error "Not ad-hoc signed: $(basename $BUNDLE)"[0m
2026-05-19T21:37:19.8869750Z [36;1m    # Allow either adhoc,runtime or just adhoc (macOS 15+ can't embed entitlements ad-hoc)[0m
2026-05-19T21:37:19.8870010Z [36;1m    if echo "$CS_INFO" | grep -q "adhoc,runtime"; then[0m
2026-05-19T21:37:19.8870240Z [36;1m      echo "  Hardened runtime: enabled"[0m
2026-05-19T21:37:19.8870360Z [36;1m    else[0m
2026-05-19T21:37:19.8870620Z [36;1m      echo "  Hardened runtime: disabled (expected — ad-hoc on macOS 15+ can't embed entitlements)"[0m
2026-05-19T21:37:19.8870880Z [36;1m    fi[0m
2026-05-19T21:37:19.8871070Z [36;1m[0m
2026-05-19T21:37:19.8871210Z [36;1m  # Verify CodeDirectory exists and is sealed[0m
2026-05-19T21:37:19.8871500Z [36;1m  echo "$CS_INFO" | grep -q "Sealed Resources" || error "Sealed Resources missing: $(basename $BUNDLE)"[0m
2026-05-19T21:37:19.8872090Z [36;1m[0m
2026-05-19T21:37:19.8872240Z [36;1m  # Check that no files are modified after signing[0m
2026-05-19T21:37:19.8872490Z [36;1m  if codesign -vvv "$BUNDLE" 2>&1 | grep -qi "modified"; then[0m
2026-05-19T21:37:19.8872740Z [36;1m    error "Files modified after signing in $(basename $BUNDLE)"[0m
2026-05-19T21:37:19.8872930Z [36;1m  fi[0m
2026-05-19T21:37:19.8873040Z [36;1mdone[0m
2026-05-19T21:37:19.8873120Z [36;1m[0m
2026-05-19T21:37:19.8873220Z [36;1mecho "Code signature: OK"[0m
2026-05-19T21:37:19.8873350Z [36;1m[0m
2026-05-19T21:37:19.8873460Z [36;1m# ============================================================[0m
2026-05-19T21:37:19.8873690Z [36;1m# 5. ENTITLEMENTS (skip if no hardened runtime — ad-hoc on macOS 15+ can't embed)[0m
2026-05-19T21:37:19.8873950Z [36;1m# ============================================================[0m
2026-05-19T21:37:19.8874110Z [36;1mecho ""[0m

2026-05-19T21:37:19.8874390Z [36;1mecho "-------------------------"[0m
2026-05-19T21:37:19.8874530Z [36;1m[0m
2026-05-19T21:37:19.8874650Z [36;1mcheck_entitlements() {[0m
2026-05-19T21:37:19.8874780Z [36;1m  local BIN="$1"[0m
2026-05-19T21:37:19.8874900Z [36;1m  local NAME="$2"[0m
2026-05-19T21:37:19.8875070Z [36;1m  local CS_INFO=$(codesign -dvv "$BIN" 2>&1 || echo "")[0m
2026-05-19T21:37:19.8875290Z [36;1m  if echo "$CS_INFO" | grep -q "runtime"; then[0m
2026-05-19T21:37:19.8875500Z [36;1m    # Hardened runtime is enabled — check entitlements[0m
2026-05-19T21:37:19.8875860Z [36;1m    local ENTITLEMENTS=$(codesign -d --entitlements - "$BIN" 2>/dev/null || echo "")[0m
2026-05-19T21:37:19.8876130Z [36;1m    if [ -z "$ENTITLEMENTS" ]; then[0m
2026-05-19T21:37:19.8876340Z [36;1m      error "No entitlements found in $NAME (has hardened runtime)"[0m
2026-05-19T21:37:19.8876560Z [36;1m    else[0m
2026-05-19T21:37:19.8876830Z [36;1m      echo "$ENTITLEMENTS" | grep -q "com.apple.security.cs.disable-library-validation" || \[0m
2026-05-19T21:37:19.8877190Z [36;1m        error "Missing disable-library-validation entitlement in $NAME"[0m
2026-05-19T21:37:19.8877420Z [36;1m    fi[0m
2026-05-19T21:37:19.8877530Z [36;1m  else[0m
2026-05-19T21:37:19.8877690Z [36;1m    echo "SKIP: $NAME has no hardened runtime — entitlements not applicable"[0m
2026-05-19T21:37:19.8877870Z [36;1m  fi[0m
2026-05-19T21:37:19.8877950Z [36;1m}[0m
2026-05-19T21:37:19.8878040Z [36;1m[0m
2026-05-19T21:37:19.8878150Z [36;1mcheck_entitlements "$VST3_BIN" "VST3"[0m
2026-05-19T21:37:19.8878330Z [36;1mcheck_entitlements "$CLAP_BIN" "CLAP"[0m
2026-05-19T21:37:19.8878470Z [36;1m[0m
2026-05-19T21:37:19.8878580Z [36;1mecho "Entitlements: OK"[0m
2026-05-19T21:37:19.8878690Z [36;1m[0m
2026-05-19T21:37:19.8878790Z [36;1m# ============================================================[0m

Actions will be forced to run with Node.js 24 by default starting June 2nd, 2026. Node.js 20 will be removed from the runner on September 16th, 2026. Please check if updated versions of these actions are available that support Node.js 24. To opt into Node.js 24 now, set the FORCE_JAVASCRIPT_ACTIONS_TO_NODE24=true environment variable on the runner or in your workflow file. Once Node.js 24 becomes the default, you can temporarily opt out by setting ACTIONS_ALLOW_USE_UNSECURE_NODE_VERSION=true. For more information see: https://github.blog/changelog/2025-09-19-deprecation-of-node-20-on-github-actions-runners/
